<Review>My family decided to give this place a try because of the high reviews.....It was dreadful. Our first pizza was burned, black edges and very dark brown crust.
When we called they said they would make us another one. When I picked up the new pizza the were completely unapologetic and condescending, opening it in my face and asking "is this one okay?" ( If you dont know the answer to that question and thought the first was good, then you shouldn't be making Pizza)
Sadly the (good) pizza wasnt good either. The crust was still overdone, dry, and tasted kind of burned. There was too much cheese distributed unevenly and caked together, but the worst part was the sauce.
I love spicy food, but you shouldnt make your base sauce too spicy that kids cant eat it, if somebody wants spicy pizza they can add red pepper.
Like some other reviews mentioned, the sauce was way too spicy for my child to eat. So after all the money spent, two trips, I still didnt have edible food for my family. TRASH, not going back.<//Review><date>1573598085820</date><user_id>105493310254979699417<//user_id>< Rating>

We are new to Chico and were referred to Chico Creek Animal Hospital by a neighbor.  We took our senior dog in for a check up and were immediately made to feel very welcome. <text>Came to Valencia to check out some cribs and things at buy buy baby. After, my family wanted to go and eat and we searched what was near by and we found this place.
We got here an hour before they close and they attended us with such a great attitude. We got nothing but the best hospitality here.

< review>
My go to favorite San Bruno Avenue tea house was unexpectedly closed üò± so I decided to try a neighboring tea house Tea Plus! Firstly, their happy hour special is a few cents cheaper than my fav place which was a instant plus in these penny pinching pandemic times! I ordered a Passion Fruit Slushy with a combination of passion fruit jellies and bobas and while not as photogenic as my favorite drink it was absolutely delish, I was munching on jellies and bobas for awhile after the drink was finished so it's safe to say the ordering of the extra combo probably was overkill. The one truly wonderful part of my visit to Tea Plus was the customer service. The older gentleman that was supervising a younger worker took over as I think my add-ons were a bit complicated to the check out app they used and he was friendly and knowledgeable and made me feel very welcome I felt that my drink choice was in truly good hands. Customer service is a rarity around SF at most times so when it is provided I'm always apppreciative! The cons would be that the ambiance is lacking and the drinks again aren't very photogenic but the pros heavily outweigh these small cons. Five star customer service and a yummy in my tummy afternoon drink! Thank you Tea Plus I will be visiting again for sure and now I have two very favorite San Bruno Avenue Tea Houses for my special treats! I think next time I'll be trying the crepes as well or maybe even the spam hand roll! *** Major plus I didn't pay an upcharge for my jelly boba combos!</review>

<Text>One blustery evening, my boo and I were exploring the streets of San Francisco. It was super late and many eateries were closing, but one little place caught our eye. Never having been there before, we decided to pop in to Tea Plus for a quick refreshing bubbly drink. They had a really extensive menu and many available toppings as well as customized ice and sweetness preferences. I ordered the chocolate coconut milk Boba drink. The drink was sweeter than pie and creamier than hell. The tapioca Boba added a nice chewy, starchy bite that hit the spot just right. Although the taste was lit AF and quenched a thirst deep within, the service was a bit odd and we had to wait around 20 minutes for a drink. We asked the server how he was doing and he responded with a phrase including a few casual obscenities, which I personally didn't mind but a straight laced professional might to take offense to such lingo. But due to the drink quality and taste, we returned twice and got the Oreo Milk Tea with Boba tapioca. Honestly best drink I've ever had, hunty. Ever since my review 8 months ago the shelves are stocked and cleaned regularly, in fact there were plenty of boxes of Pokemon TCG that were quite a few generations back so we were able to finish our collections without paying surcharged prices due to the age of generation. The boxes of stock have been moved out of the front checkout area of the collectibles aisle. The bathrooms have been cleaned up as well which is a major plus for me. Customer service is still great. And the helpfullness and stock is always above and beyond. Thanks Target!

Target is a convenient place for me to shop when I need to grab baby items, groceries, and a few other miscellaneous items. This Target in particular is easy to navigate and generally well stocked with the items I need. However, there are a couple area's that could use some improvement. For instance, you can tell when an area has been given a blind eye due to it's location, my husband collects Pokemon cards and it seems that the two areas that carry these cards are hardly stocked, usually disheveled with card packs not being in the right place, and cramped with empty boxes or carts strewn about the aisles and shelves. I could understand packs not being on the right hooks because there are usually children who look through these, however when your shopping experience is hindered because you have to sift through empty boxes, or push multiple carts out of an already cramped space it makes it feel like you went into the backroom where the stock is kept, and to see the same mess on different days, it makes you wonder if they give any attention to these two locations. Secondly, the bathrooms are always a wreck. I have never seen restrooms so messed up. Again, I can understand after a rush, or maybe because of the holidays, but again when you come to your local Target and see the same mess over several days it makes you wonder how much time they devote to such a private and public place.
